## [ADAM] 2026-04-13 10:30 | UK UAT - SE 2026-04 Launch (30 min)
**With:** Mitchell Payne;Bethany Sullivan;Liam Bond;Josh Sullivan;Amy Banes;Adam Martin;Bradley Roots;Alice Maghie;Laura Maddocks;

```
Meeting to discuss the launch of 2026-04 to beta.

Following direction from Amy, we will be changing our JIRA system again to fall in line with a global initiative to make UAT testing consistent across regions. We will have a single epic representing the UAT cycle with subtasks/linked tickets to structure the testing. The single ticket will also have a checklist for things like submission testing, Cloudbridge and Sync TB tests etc, so we are certain and things are clear.

I am off the week leading up to this, as we don't know the contents yet I can't prepare the ticket and tasks until the day of meeting. I will aspire to get things set up before this call but who knows.

We need to review the SE notes and ensure we know who will have testing tasks for the new features, and also consider any SE Builder, DA, Collaborate or iXBRL announcements/notes that might come out in the meantime.

🚀 Caseware Hackathon: Innovation in Action Kick Off

 

The Hackathon is here! — and whether you're in the building or not, you’re invited to be part of the excitement!

Join us on October 7th as we kick off this company wide event and start what can only be described as 2 days of friendly, competitive, determined competition to come up with the best innovation hack possible!

From Oct 7–8, teams across Caseware will be exploring bold ideas powered by AI. 

Join us again on Thursday, Oct 9, to watch the live judging and see what the teams have created, and who the winners are!

## [WILL] 2025-04-29 12:00 | Sync TB work (30 min)
**With:** Mitchell Payne;David Garcia;Jonathan Millar;Liam Bond;Will Walker;

```
Sync TB works by connecting a "parent" engagement to a "child" engagement, where the child receives the TB from the parent.  In order for this to be mapped correctly, we have to deploy a mapping config file to the mono repo of the child engagement's app.

In the UK's case, all parent apps will be financials, and all child apps will be audit. This means that only Audit needs to deploy these mapping files to their apps' mono repos

This meeting is to organise this and deploy as needed.
